 chaar maichon kii shrunkhlaa main bhartiya team 1-0 se aage he
 The fate of all the candidates for the 16th Lok Sabha will be decided on Friday with the opening of EVM machines
 iske liye iviem mashiinon kii sahi tarah se sil hona behad ahm hoga, taaki nishpakshtapurvak matganana ho sake
 The green seal will be the most important in these machines, which will know whether the machine has been tampered with or not
 darasal, jis prakaar matpeti ko band karne ke liye hare rang kii paper sil hoti he, usee prakaar electranik matdaan mashin ke control unit ko bhi band karne ke liye hare rang kii paper sil hi ekmaatr mahatvapurn sil hoti he
 If these green paper seals are intact then there can be no rigging in the control unit and there will be no effect in the recording of votes by the machine
 vahiin, koi sil jaise control unit ke kairing bakse kii sil yaa ummidavaar set khand kii sil yaa parinaam khand kii sil kshatigrast pai jaati he, lekin hare rang kii paper sil barkaraar he to matdaan centre kaa matdaan kaa parinaam janaa ja saktaa he
 Instructions have been given about the counting of votes on Friday that if the green paper seals are not found the same, then the control unit will be kept separate and the results of the votes recorded in that unit will not be counted
 jila nirvachan adhikari rajasekhar ne kaha he ki matganana ke liye hare rang kii paper sil kii mahatta dekhte hue ummidavaar or unke gananaa agenton ko is baat se santusht hone ke liye uchit avasar dena chahie
 They could be satisfied that the paper seal is the same as that put by the presiding officer at the polling station before the commencement of polling
 bhartiya janata party ke pradhanmantri pad ke ummidavaar narendra modi do siton se chunaav maidan main utarane ko taiyaar hai
 If party sources are to be believed, it is almost decided that Modi will contest from Vadodara seat in Gujarat along with Varanasi
 bijepi kii aaj kendriya chunaav samiti kii baithak he jiske baad modi ko vadodara se pratyaashee ghoshit kiya ja saktaa he

 isamen gujarat ke pratyaashiyon kaa bhi elaan kiya jayega, jiske baad saaf ho jayega ki varisht bijepi netaa laal krishna adwani kahaan se chunaav ladenge

 phukare kaa chuuchaa yani varuna sharma ek baar phir chhichhore banakar darshakon ko hansaaenge
 During a conversation with Naveen Kumar in Mumbai, he spoke to Babaki on issues other than 'chhichhore'
 pesh hai mukhya ansh-mumbai
 Varun Sharma, who makes the world laugh, is also scared
 unka yah dar thodaa alag he
 They say, 'I do not want to let my loved ones break the hope that they have set with me, that is, they want to laugh
 meri bhi yah koshish he ki jab bhi wo mujhe dekhen to unke chehre par muskuraahat ho
 After Fukrey Ka Chucha, Varun Sharma, Arjun Patiala and Khandani Shafakhana, Chichhore will once again make the audience laugh with his interesting character in the film
 
 He says, 'my character's name is Seksa and this seksa does such things that people will laugh and laugh
 ' dangal fame nirdeshak nitesh tiwari ne is film kaa nirdesan kiya he
 It also stars Sushant Singh Rajput and Shraddha Kapoor
 shraddha kii abhi saaho relies hui he or log unhen pasand kar rahe hai
 Chichore can get the benefit of this
 varuna ne chhichhore main nitesh se abhinay kii alag vidha bhi sikhi he
 Varun feels that comedy is the most difficult genre in acting
 logon ko lagata he ki hansaana sabase aasaan he
 But this is the most difficult thing
 aaj aisa samay he ki har koi pareshaan he or har koi duusare ko pareshaan bhi kar detaa he
 We are engaged in our struggle and also in the running of life
 isse dhairya kam ho gaya he
 If you can make someone laugh for a short time, then it is very good
 lekin kamedi film main ek banda hansaane kaa kaam akelaa nahin kar saktaa
 It is very important to get the team right
 main kitna bhi acha seen kar duun, agar saamne se riection nahin aayaa to wo seen aapako bor kar degaa
 It is necessary to match the timing with the action
 phukare se apni safalataa kii gaadi par savaar varuna kamedi ke liye tipcast hone se bor nahin hote hai
 As Varun, 'I cannot be bored as long as the audience is getting a dose of laughter from me
 mujhe bhi acha lag rahaa he ki main regular basis par cast ho rahaa hum kamedi joner main
 It is important for me to cast on a regular basis, be typecast later
 main bhi is cheez ko enjvaay karata hum
 It feels good to laugh logon ko muskuraate dekhnaa acha lagata he
 By the way, Varun is also waiting for a script which is of a different genre
 ve kehete hai, 'main alag shed vaali ek film main kaam kar rahaa hum jiskaa naam he ruh afja
 It is a horror comedy
 isamen kamedi to he hi, alag joner bhi saath he horer kaa
 Scare and scare will make you laugh and scare you
 'varuna bataate hai ki phukare se pehle unhone kabhi bhi kamedi karne kaa prayaas nahin kiya tha
 Because before that he used to do serious plays like Ashwatthama and Andhayug in Chandigarh
 paanch saal tak theatre karne ke baad phukare ke audishan ke samay pehali baar kamedi karne kaa prayaas kiya tha
 When he saw the film, he felt that he could make people laugh
 ve kehete hai, 'jindagi main aisa change aayaa ki phukare ke baad joner hi kamedi ban gaya
 But i miss the theater
 mauka mila to kabhi ek play jarur karuunga
 "there is no need to imitate anyone for comedy
" ' varuna aage kehete hai, 'ab sichuational kamedi he
 i like Charlie Chaplin very much
 maine unki sari filmein dekhi he
 But my acting will not get his mark
 ' bataur varuna, 'main jab bhi koi bhi siries dekhtaa hum to usamen kamedi nahin dekhtaa hum
 i watch such things as thriller, Dark
 thri percent, blike mirar meraa pasandida sho he
 i do not watch standup comedy
 mujhe kya hansaata he yah pataa nahin
